Personal Settings

Personal rules (@rcmdnk) Import
For HHKB ((Shift-)Esc to grave accent (tilde))
iTerm2 command (Meta) keys
ESC (or Control-[) sends ESC EISU ESC
Copy and Paste, ctrl-z/x/c/v to cmd-z/x/c/v
Next/Prev by ctrl-i/o, option-left/right arrow
Browsers (cmd-(shift-)tab to cmd-opt-right(left))
Microsoft Office (ctrl-h, font, superscript/subscript)
Change cmd-ctrl-h/j/k/l to arrow keys
Window Actions
Mouse cursor move
Control-[ to ESC
Others (Dock, Sleep, Delete, IME, Misison Control, Spotlight)

For HHKB ((Shift-)Esc to grave accent (tilde))

  • Only for HHKB (vendor id = 2131).
  • And only for terminal, vim, emacs.
  • As HHKB's ESC is place for ` (gravce accent (back quote)) and ~ (tilde) at other keyboards.
  • Better to bind Control-[ to ESC as in below setting.
Key bindings
escape grave_accent_and_tilde

iTerm2 command (Meta) keys

  • Command to Option (i.e. Meta key) for other than n, v, w.

ESC (or Control-[) sends ESC EISU ESC

  • For terminal, vim, emacs.
  • Send ESC, EISU and ESC to stop changing at IME, disable IME and change to Normal mode at Vim at once.
  • Need to disable ESC at copy mode if GNU screen is used. Add following line in your .screenrc to disable ESC at copy mode:
    bindkey -m ^[ eval ''
Key bindings
escape escape, japanese_eisuu, escape
control-open_bracket escape, japanese_eisuu, escape

Copy and Paste, ctrl-z/x/c/v to cmd-z/x/c/v

  • For other than terminal, vim, emacs.
  • Copy and Paste with control key.
Key bindings
control-z command-z
control-x command-x
control-c command-c
control-v command-v

Next/Prev by ctrl-i/o, option-left/right arrow

  • For other than terminal, vim, emacs.
Key bindings
control-i command-close_bracket
control-o command-open_bracket
option-right_arrow command-close_bracket
option-left_arrow command-open_bracket

Browsers (cmd-(shift-)tab to cmd-opt-right(left))

  • For Firefox, Chrome, Safari.
Key bindings
command-tab command-option-right_arrow
command-shift-tab command-option-left_arrow

Microsoft Office (ctrl-h, font, superscript/subscript)

Change cmd-ctrl-h/j/k/l to arrow keys

  • Vim like move.

Window Actions

  • Window actions with AppleScript.
  • Need [rcmdnk/AppleScript](https://github.com/rcmdnk/AppleScript) to be installed.
Key bindings
command-4 shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/close.scpt
control-4 shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/close.scpt
control-command-a shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/closeToDock.scpt

control-shift-i shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/windowMoveUp.scpt
control-shift-o shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/windowMoveRight.scpt

Mouse cursor move

  • Need [rcmdnk/AppleScript](https://github.com/rcmdnk/AppleScript) to be installed.
  • Need to enable Mouse Key from System Preferences→Accessibility→Mouse and Trackpad.
Key bindings
control-shift-h shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/mouseMoveLeft.scpt
control-shift-j shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/mouseMoveDown.scpt
control-shift-k shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/mouseMoveUp.scpt
control-shift-l shell_command: osascript ~/Library/Scripts/mouseMoveRight.scpt
control-shift-n button1
control-shift-m button3
control-shift-p button2
